Free Talk

A Word or Two 233

— Wang Zongzhou

True love often leads to tragic dramas.

The joy of marriage is far less than the joy of divorce.

A woman feels humiliated when oppressed by a man, while a man feels honored when oppressed by a woman.

If school authorities forbid students from exchanging love letters, then Chinese language teachers will have nothing to eat.

Being in the whirlpool of love is like hovering between heaven and hell.

If you fail at something, as long as you struggle with the cause of the failure, you can eventually succeed.

When striving forward, you must not look back, but after reaching your goal, you must look back.

Changing one's tune due to attacks from public opinion shows a complete lack of understanding of the true meaning of love.

The source of suicide often flows with women who are rich in emotion.

A Brief Stay at Mogan Mountain (3) 234

— Jingbo

The number of visitors to the mountains this summer to escape the heat has increased several times compared to last year. There are reasons for this. The current situation is turbulent, and the clouds of war are looming. Mount Lu is in a dangerous area, and Western merchants who had appointments there cannot travel. Many of them come to the mountains together. In previous years, Westerners from Shanghai thought that the three islands of Japan were beautiful, and they lingered in Hakone and Unzen. Now, because silver is cheap and gold is expensive, it is difficult to expect a reservation. Therefore, tourists flock to Mogan Mountain, reaching a peak for a time. In terms of accommodation in the mountains, besides the railway hotel, Westerners mostly rent houses. After I went to Hangzhou, I learned that there were no more rooms available in the hotel, so I dared not go to the mountains hastily. Later, after several telegrams with the China Travel Service, I finally got a place to stay. After this, I saw several guests come to the mountains, but they left after a meal because there were no more rooms available, which was also disappointing. The best things in the mountains are bamboo and springs. Bamboo is everywhere in the mountains, and the springs are also tinkling and pleasant to the ear. The scenery in the morning and evening is also constantly changing, making it impossible to explore. Zhou Mengpo has an article describing the scenery of the mountains, saying, "Mogan Mountain was named in the Zhou Dynasty because the King of Wu cast swords there. The peaks stand tall and can reach the sky. Sometimes thunder rumbles underfoot, and clouds rise in the urn. Sometimes springs fly from outside the sky, and waterfalls fall by the pillow. In the morning, sweat flows and fans are waved. In the evening, clothes are thin and cotton is put on. As Su Dongpo said, 'I do not know the true face of Mount Lu.' It is not that one does not really know it, but that it changes in an instant, and everything is shifted by the wind and clouds. Mogan Mountain is also like this. The mountains are planted with bamboo, tall, low, big, and small, each gathered by type, connecting the mountains and bordering the territory, not just thousands of acres of the Wei River. This is what Mount Lu, Beidaihe, and Chicken Foot Mountain cannot match. It is worth the travel of people from China and abroad who admire it with their hearts and focus on it with their eyes." I stayed in the mountains for a short time and never waved a fan or sweated. The so-called sweat flowing and fans being waved in the morning is not entirely true. However, Mengpo's article describes the scenery of the mountains in great detail.

A Glimpse of the Tragic Situation of the People of Henan 235

— Rouyun

The Central Plains of Henan was right in the path of the North-South war. Since the Republic, there has hardly been a day of peace. In addition to the disasters of war, there have been natural disasters. Recently, a friend came from Kaifeng and described the tragic situation there as follows. Hearing it in Shanghai made my heart ache, and I grieved for my compatriots, who have no way to live. Therefore, I will describe the outline of the situation below to tell the people of the country.

Flies as Big as Bees: For now, let us leave aside the war and only discuss the natural disasters. This alone is enough to drain the marrow and blood of the people of Henan, and there is more than enough left. Locusts and incessant rain followed the war. The fields were barren and the land was red for thousands of miles. Poor families had not heard of rice and wheat for years. They dug up grass roots and tree bark to eat, but even the grass roots and tree bark were almost completely dug up. Large families, in order to maintain their lives, had to sell their sons and daughters for one or two yuan in order to seek a full meal. Flesh and blood were scattered and turned in the ditches. The tragic situation was like this. Since the beginning of summer, a kind of fly as big as a bee has suddenly been discovered in the area along the Longhai Railway war zone. The body structure of the fly is no different from the usual ones, but the body of the fly is especially large and has a needle-like sting like a bee. According to those who know, this kind of large fly is formed by the bones and blood of the dead rotting on the sand field. The flies first appeared near the battlefield and then spread everywhere, with the sting causing pain that pierces the heart and lungs. Some people in Henan hide in small rooms all day long to avoid the poisonous sting, which is also said to be suffering.

Four County Magistrates in One County: In addition to suffering from this kind of insect poison, the people of Henan also suffer from so-called human poison, which is an even more substantial pain. When troops pass through a county, they must carry out a looting. After satisfying their desires, they set off. The troops in Henan are no different from locusts on rice. If looting is not enough, they will appoint their own trusted county magistrates as a means of collecting taxes. When Team A passes through, they appoint B as the county magistrate. When Team C passes through, they appoint D as the county magistrate. A certain county, known for its fertility, now has four different county magistrates. When a new county magistrate takes office, there must be a new arrangement. Various taxes are levied under cleverly established names, which are too many to count. Each county magistrate has their own method of collecting money. Political orders come from many sources, and there is nowhere to turn. Human poison is also very terrible.

Rouyun Said: The people of Henan are suffering like water that is deep and fire that is hot. The people of that place are looking forward to the arrival of government troops to alleviate their suffering. I deeply hope that the anti-rebel soldiers at the front will bravely advance and save the people of Henan from the fire and water.

Movies in the Sweltering Heat 236

— Jiade

The summer heat torments people, and it is difficult to pass the long days. Preparing ice and cutting melons can alleviate the heat a little, but the mental fatigue is really impossible to get rid of. I am addicted to the cinema and only use watching movies to amuse myself. The Shanghai cinemas that have air conditioning equipment are the Nanjing and Guanglu theaters. However, staying there for only two hours is very cool, but when you come out of the theater, you feel the heat even more intensely. For outdoor movies at night, the time is not suitable. I heard that the business of cinemas declines during the summer because they are all affected by the weather.

However, the excitement of enjoying a good film is still strong. I remember when the film "Laihun" was screened for the second time, it was also in the height of summer, but the seats were full. Even though we were sweating profusely, we didn't feel the heat. Especially the snow and ice scenes in the film made people unintentionally forget the heat outside the theater and feel like they were enjoying the coolness in the film. Thinking about it now, I still have a lingering taste. Also, I went to see the film "The Gold Rush" several times. When it was screened in Beijing last summer, it was still full. In the midst of laughter, I saw the snow scenes and didn't feel the bleak and desolate background. Otherwise, watching a film of the Great War, on the battlefield and under the artillery fire, you would feel like you were there and would be unbearable.

Many of the recent domestic films are action films. The shadows of swords and the light of knives are extremely tense, but watching them in the summer heat always feels unpleasant. I heard that the Mingxing Film Company has recently produced a long film "Taohua Lake," directed by Mr. Zheng Zhengqiu. The film describes an emotional story in a sorrowful tone, and it is more subtle and delicate than the films "Baiyun Pagoda" and "Meihua Luo." The first episode of the film depicts exotic scenery, using Kulun as the background. The snowy landscape is full of poetic meaning, and the scenery is rarely seen on such a grand scale. I heard that the film has been completed and will be screened soon. The silver light and snow shadows should be able to dispel the accumulated heat in the heart.

I remember that Soreen Play magazine once published a June special issue, in which the text and pictures were all taken from the lives of movie stars escaping the summer heat and the snow and ice scenes in the films. Holding one in hand, you can forget the afternoon fatigue. It can be seen that when watching movies in the summer, the background of the film should be taken into consideration.

A Primary School Teacher Who Sells Toads 237

— Long

Can Earn 4,000 Wen Per Day

In recent years, primary school teachers in various places have taken up side jobs such as pulling rickshaws and barbering because their salaries are too low to maintain their livelihoods. Such reports have been published in the newspapers from time to time, and those who see them all use them as conversation pieces. However, there has been no one like Mr. Zhu of our county (Nanhui) who specializes in selling toads as a way to make money, which is especially unique. I will briefly outline the situation below to tell those who care about education and people's livelihood issues.

Zhu Huisheng of Shenzhuang Town, Nanhui County, is a certified teacher. According to the regulations of the Education Bureau of our county, all certified teachers receive a third-class salary of 18 yuan per month, including food expenses. In this era of rising prices, the price of rice has risen to more than 20 yuan per stone. Without being intelligent, one would know that it is difficult to use this small income to provide for the clothing and food of oneself and one's family. Mr. Zhu, realizing that the bread problem has entered a dangerous situation and that the solution cannot be delayed, resolutely abandoned his important responsibility of cultivating the future masters of the country. Every day, he goes barefoot to the fields to catch a large number of toads, cuts them open, skins them, washes them in clean water, and adds five books of Chen wine, soy sauce, and other ingredients to cook them in a pot. He carries them to various towns to sell. The people in the market compete to buy them because they are fat, tender, and delicious, no less than frog meat. According to what Mr. Zhu told people, he can earn a net profit of more than 4,000 wen per day, which is more than double the salary of a teacher. Long believes that Mr. Zhu is able to adapt to circumstances and open up new ways of making money, which is a wise thing to do. But I don't know what kind of new plans he will invent when there is a shortage of toads in the future, which makes other teachers who value their status and are rigid and uncompromising feel pitiful as they sit in their sorrowful cities all day long.

Trivial Notes from Dancheng 238

— Liu Mengdie

It has been several years since my footsteps last trod Dancheng. In the last days of the seventh month of this year, I was wearily suffering from summer heat in Xishan, when Lin Youmei, a fellow townsman, urgently invited me with a specially delivered letter to the inaugural exhibition of the Qingyun Calligraphy and Painting Society, which he had founded, hoping for me to take a look. Moved by his friendship, my homesickness stirred, and I mustered the courage to embark on the journey. It was deep into the night when I arrived, as the train I took that day was delayed along the way, nominally an express train but actually exceptionally slow. The night was pitch black, and the station had poor lighting. After getting off, I groped my way to the city gate before finally finding a rickshaw puller, boarded his rickshaw, and went straight to the residence of my old friend Jiang Mengfei on Taiping Bridge. Having not visited for several years, I was quite disoriented. Initially, I intended to get off at the bridge, but I traveled for a long time without seeing it. Upon asking the locals, I learned that Taiping Bridge had already been leveled. It turned out that Taiping was originally a dry bridge, and it was removed to prevent traffic obstruction. This is a small example of the changes of hills and valleys, a minor vicissitude of life.

The next morning, Mengfei and two other guests accompanied me to the society to meet the society head, Youmei, and his elder brother Youyun. They then led me to the exhibition, which was held in the silk shop guild hall at Ma Lane Gate. The day was the height of the summer heat, and I sweated profusely, finding it unbearable. However, the hall's buildings were tall and spacious, providing a cool respite from the heat, as it was the former residence of the local gentry, the Shu family. However, in a short time, my emotions were stirred, as the displayed calligraphy and paintings by famous artists numbered over two hundred pieces, all collected and mounted by Youmei alone, forming this grand spectacle. His grand ambition and perseverance are truly astonishing and admirable. Although I have dabbled in calligraphy in recent years, haphazardly painting here and there, I have never truly practiced the fundamentals and do not have confidence in my skills. However, there are many who appreciate my works, mistakenly lauding my reputation, and constantly requesting my services. Writing fans during the summer season is an especially timely task. Often, wherever I go, I am sweating and working. Among the exhibits, there is also a scroll of cursive script, only displayed because the society head admired it and would not allow me to hide my inadequacies. The Lin brothers also hosted a banquet at the exhibition, extending the utmost hospitality. As a wanderer far from home, finding myself unable to return home, I was able to gather with these old friends and new acquaintances, and my feelings of gratitude and comfort were beyond description.

On the day of departure, I made a small detour to visit an acquaintance. The brief visit inadvertently stirred old feelings, giving me a sense of Du Mu's experience in Huzhou. The beautiful maiden of the past has now become a modern middle-aged woman, her children grown. It is as the saying goes, "Green leaves become shade, branches full of offspring." I also recalled Yan Jidao's poem "Partridge Sky," with the line "Still fearing that meeting is but a dream." The situation was somewhat similar, so I composed a poem in the same meter: "Remembering the beautiful lady in her boudoir, singularly favored, her face like a delicate peach blossom, a deep red. The old promise before the flowers, a spring dream returning. Coming again outside the gate, I sadly lament the evening breeze. Not daring to meet, yet meeting unexpectedly, shocked by the haggard appearance at this moment. Pitying the itinerant lover on the road, on leaving, a warm smile lingering."

New Knowledge for the Family 239

— Compiled by Tianxu Wosheng

I once read an article in a commercial journal stating that magnesium carbonate could extinguish fire, but I did not take it to heart. During the Lantern Festival, at a makeup pavilion in Huayuqi, a table was set up near the bed, with a carpet laid on the floor. The table was covered with a cloth blanket, and there was barely any space for the dishes and plates. The food was abundant, and the guests were all good drinkers, so the cups were filled with brandy. Each person's place setting also had a wrinkled paper printed handkerchief, folded into the shape of a concentric square knot. The electric lamp was covered with a large silk shade, adorned with red silk tassels, hanging low near the table, no more than three feet above. The waiter brought in a chrysanthemum hotpot, pouring flaming liquor into it. Unexpectedly, the flame ignited the bottle in his hand, causing him to panic and release it. The flaming liquor and bottle landed on the table, causing a fire. The dishes and bowls overturned, and the brandy fueled the flames. If it spread to the floor, the carpet and bed curtains would also catch fire, and the danger was overwhelming. I then noticed a long tube of toothpaste on the dressing table, remembering that magnesium carbonate could reduce fire. I sprinkled it onto the table, and wherever the powder landed, the flames were immediately extinguished, covering all areas, high and low, effectively stopping the disaster. The people in the house fetched water, originally intending to put out the fire, but instead used it to wash the cups and refill them. The remaining food and wine were removed for the servants to enjoy, who praised it and said it had a unique fragrance and was even more delicious. My family used to buy only a few tubes of toothpaste, but after this incident, we now buy a dozen tubes each time and distribute them to each room as insurance. The uses of the "Invincible" brand toothpaste do not mention this function. Is it just a coincidence? (Canghaisheng) Xu writes: The main components of fire extinguishing powder are magnesium carbonate and boric acid. However, toothpaste is light, and when used in the aforementioned situation, it can extinguish fire. For fire protection, it is still advisable to purchase fire extinguishing powder or a fire hose.

Impressions of a Trip to the East (24) 240

— Qian Hua

(18) The Cost of Living in Tokyo

As material civilization progresses, the cost of living increases. Tokyo is the center of Japanese politics and culture, so the cost of living there is almost on par with Europe and America. Generally, families with a monthly income of 300 Japanese yen or more can barely maintain their living expenses. Housewives personally handle most of the chores, and they live in simple rented houses with few amenities. Otherwise, even a little extravagance will lead to debt. To get to work at companies and associations every day, long-distance trains and public buses are used as convenient modes of transportation. Otherwise, people walk. Cars are hardly considered an option for commuting to work. As for the lower classes, students, and laborers, their lives are supported by the social welfare programs of the social bureaus and the authorities, such as simple canteens and public housing, which are priced very low. Therefore, a minimum income of about 70-80 Japanese yen is enough to support a family and keep them adequately fed. Since the lifting of the gold embargo, the Japanese authorities have adopted a tight monetary policy, doing everything possible to lower the cost of living. The government's power is used to force stores to lower the prices of everyday goods. Therefore, within Japan, the general cost of living has gradually decreased. However, Chinese residents still find it very difficult to live in Tokyo due to the high exchange rate (two Chinese yuan equals about one Japanese yen). The Japanese admire European culture in everything. Eight or nine out of ten men wear Western suits. Japanese also incorporates many English words, and specialized terms are still called by their original English names. Hotel furnishings are purely Western style, with wooden beds, desks, and chairs, similar to the exquisite hotels in China, collectively called "Hoteiru," the transliteration of the English word "Hotel." Ordinary hotel room rates start at three Japanese yen per day and can go up to twenty or thirty yen. Meals are available in the attached dining rooms, which offer both Western and Japanese cuisine for guests to choose from. Breakfast costs one Japanese yen, lunch costs one yen and twenty cents, and dinner costs one yen and a half. Therefore, in terms of food and lodging alone, the average traveler must spend more than ten yen per day. The Imperial Hotel in Tokyo is the most famous, and is frequented by high-ranking officials and wealthy merchants, who spend dozens or even hundreds of yen per day, which is not surprising. There is also a purely Japanese-style inn, where food and lodging are cheaper. The rooms are covered with tatami mats, and the room rate depends on the number of mats. There is a public bathhouse where male and female guests bathe together in the same pool, revealing every detail of their curves. Japanese are used to it and are calm. If Chinese people were to see this, it would be considered a strange tale. There are boundaries in the room. In the Hotel, the bathroom is separate, there is no such pleasure. The Japanese like to be clean and bathe at least once a day. Most middle-class families have their own bathrooms, while ordinary people go to the public bathhouse in the city, which costs only five cents. However, soap and towels must be brought. Men and women are in the same pool, separated by a thin board, which is only a few feet high. If you stand on tiptoe, you can see the naked beauty in full view.

Eastern Tour Correspondence (15) 241

— Wu Xiaohou

(4) Town Council Expenses

The expenses of the town council vary depending on the size of the area and the amount of funding required. Generally, there are office expenses, transportation subsidies, sanitation expenses, night watch expenses, congratulatory and condolence expenses, festival expenses, and other miscellaneous items. The largest, such as the Aoyama North and South 6-chome Association in Akasaka Ward, has an annual total of 4,472.647 yen. The smallest, such as the Garyu-cho Town Council in Koishikawa Ward, has an annual total of 1,200 yen. The number of members varies, and the most expensive, such as the Koji 5-chome Self-Defense Association in Kojimachi Ward, costs 41.855 yen per member per year. The least expensive, such as the Minami-Iga-cho Town Council in Yotsuya Ward, costs 1.874 yen per member per year.

(5) Town Council Sanitation Association

In Meiji 30, the Japanese government promulgated the Infectious Disease Prevention Law. In February of the 33rd year, the Tokyo Prefecture re-promulgated the regulations for the establishment of sanitation associations. Each town council then established a sanitation association. Among the 15 wards of Tokyo City, excluding Honjo Ward, which is still being organized due to special circumstances, Kojimachi has 8 groups, Kanda has 18 groups, Nihonbashi has 130 groups, Kyobashi has 16 groups, Shiba Ward has 7 groups, Azabu has 20 groups, Akasaka has 1 group, Yotsuya has 58 groups, Ushigome and Koishikawa each have 26 groups, Hongo has 38 groups, Shitaya has 2 groups, Asakusa has 97 groups, and Fukagawa has 1 group, for a total of 445 groups. The most is Nihonbashi Ward, and the least are Akasaka and Fukayama Wards.

(6) Town Council Election Campaigns

Elections for members of the House of Representatives, prefectural assembly members, city council members, and ward assembly members in Japan are all based on the town council as the basic unit of election campaigns. The town council is a small regional community with intimate and mutual assistance. In the past, feelings of affection and mutual assistance were strong, and election campaigns were intimate and easy to succeed. However, in China, the representative system is often criticized for money-based election campaigns. It is not known that election campaigns in Japan, in addition to publicity, are also centered on money. It is said that in the previous election of the House of Representatives, a certain lawyer spent tens of thousands of yen, and the publicity expenses alone were more than 20,000 yen. After the election failed, he fled and his whereabouts are unknown. This kind of money-based election campaign has the same drawbacks as in China. However, the country has a special advantage, that is, in the election competition, although each party does its best, when the election results show that one party has won and the other has failed, the losing party can put the overall national situation first and submit, without insidious sabotage, so that the country's political tranquility is not disturbed. This is why Japan's national strength has been steadily increasing and is following in the footsteps of Europe and the United States to become a strong country in East Asia after the Restoration.

(7) Town Council Federation

In order to facilitate the handling of affairs and expand mutual assistance, town councils have formed town council federations. There are three types of federations: (1) Federation of all town councils within a ward; (2) Federation of town councils from different wards; (3) Federation of town councils with similar primary affairs.

Business of the American Cotton Cooperative 254

Last year, the American government established the Agricultural Bureau and organized the American Cotton Cooperative to maintain cotton prices. The authority of the Agricultural Bureau and the contents of the cooperative have been previously reported in this newspaper. The contents of the cooperative are particularly noteworthy. According to the "International Cotton Quarterly," Mr. Nodington, President of the Alabama American Cotton Cooperative, wrote an article entitled "The American Cotton Cooperative," which is translated directly below to observe its content. The American Cotton Cooperative is a national organization of cotton cooperatives, recognized by the Federal Agricultural Bureau, and its form is also approved by the Agricultural Bureau. The cooperative's authorized capital is 30 million yuan, and according to its articles of association, it may act as the general sales manager for the cotton sales of its members' marketing organizations. All cotton cooperatives, except for the Greenwood Standard Cotton Cooperative in Mississippi, are members and beneficiaries of the cooperative's achievements. For the sake of analysis, the cooperative's business can be divided into three different types.

(1) As the national cotton cooperative is the central organization for cotton cooperative members, it directly promotes the sale of all cotton owned by its branches. As the Agricultural Bureau uses financial cooperation to manage the cotton cooperative business, it provides loans to cooperative members for the following purposes: A. Lending to maintain the market, that is, state cooperatives provide loans to cotton farmers when they deliver cotton. B. Lending to state cooperatives to purchase material conveniences, such as purchasing warehouses, packing plants, and cotton gins. C. Lending to state cooperatives to subscribe to stocks of agricultural product lending companies. However, the cooperative should not lend to lending companies for the purpose of agricultural product lending, as such funds must come from third-party lending institutions or commercial banks. The scale of the lending relationship between the national cotton cooperative and state cooperatives depends on the need for funds and the collateral that state cooperatives can submit to the cooperative and the Agricultural Bureau. The affairs of the national cooperative will also realize the Agricultural Bureau's policy of organizing, educating, and cooperating among cotton planters, bankers, and merchants, and other key measures that are essential for the success of the entire movement. This type of business has the following key points related to the public: (1) Expanding the number of members of state cooperatives; (2) Striving to make American cotton production correspond to world demand in terms of quantity; (3) Improving the quality of American cotton to maintain the superiority of American cotton production and to seek the highest possible price commensurate with the quality of American cotton for cotton planters.

(2) The American Cotton Cooperative will buy and sell cotton. Whenever the cooperative and the authorities of the Agricultural Bureau believe that it is necessary to correct any errors in the cotton belt or that it is extremely beneficial to the members, the cooperative will buy and sell cotton based on the total contribution of all state branches. In other words, any private cotton merchant may buy and sell cotton domestically or abroad, or buy and sell spot cotton or futures cotton. The American Cotton Cooperative also has this right to buy and sell. When it is necessary to correct market conditions caused by manipulated or unevenly positioned long or short positions, the cooperative headquarters can deliver or take delivery of cotton on any futures market. Whether the cooperative will exercise this power and to what extent will be decided on a case-by-case basis.

(3) The primary task of the American Cotton Cooperative is to act in concert with the Agricultural Bureau in the name of a legally established cotton industry maintenance association. The maintenance function is only intended to be exercised when the situation is urgent, market conditions are special, and supply and demand and prices are affected. According to the provisions of this law, the general cooperative can use the financial assistance of the Agricultural Bureau to purchase and store cotton on the cotton market in an amount sufficient to stabilize the market price.

If cotton farmers insist on planting more cotton fields and harvesting more cotton, the Agricultural Bureau will naturally not be able to protect prices forever, and it will not be able to maintain them for a considerable period of time. This is a simple matter of reason. If the climate is very good, the cotton crop is very smooth, and the yield per acre is extraordinarily high, the Agricultural Bureau can certainly help cotton farmers to avoid bankruptcy due to the abundance of cotton harvests and to maintain the position of sellers. However, if the number of cotton fields exceeds the bounds of conservative reason, resulting in an extraordinarily abundant harvest, the Agricultural Bureau has long warned cotton farmers that in the event of such a situation, the bureau will be economically powerless to help. It is easier to limit excessive planting beforehand than to deal with it afterwards. Those with knowledge can understand this. Therefore, the Agricultural Bureau and the Cooperative are now requesting planters and those involved in the southern cotton industry to cooperate with them to reduce cotton planting, and at the same time, these two organizations are also requesting planters to produce high-quality cotton in all cotton planting areas of the South. This is because this measure is not only related to the value of the 1930 cotton crop, but also to the level of future cotton crop values and the prosperity or decline of the general cotton industry. What is now sought from the people in the national cotton industry is to unite with each other to become a whole, organized South to produce cotton, the quantity and quality of which must be most suitable for the needs of the world, and to sell their products in a way that obtains the highest possible selling price commensurate with world commercial conditions and cotton supply. (Agricultural)

Flour Market Falls Again

Export Rumors Not Yet Realized

Factory Owners Liquidate Long Positions

After the market opened yesterday morning, the current month's flour saw short covering due to outside speculators fearing that flour exports would be implemented in the future, which would inevitably cause squeezes. However, the market loosened afterwards as factory owners had differing opinions. Those who were bullish were still thinking of raising prices using the export rumors, while those who were bearish thought that the matter was just a rumor and that implementation would be difficult, so they continued to liquidate positions. When the market opened in the afternoon, small and medium-sized factory owners were still liquidating positions, and inland long positions also took the opportunity to liquidate, so prices fell again. Looking ahead, if exports are still pending, the market must continue to fluctuate and it will be difficult to fall. It is estimated that the number of autumn silkworms raised this year will be more than double the amount of spring cocoons.

Banks Closed, No Silk or Yarn Market 264

Yesterday (the 4th) was the summer holiday period for local Chinese and foreign banks, and foreign firms also followed the example and stopped operations. There was no silk or yarn market at all.

Piece Goods and Cotton Cloth See Excellent Sales 265

Eastern Goods Arrive in Force, Prices Fall Step by Step

Yangtze River Trade Plummets

Local Cotton Cloth 266

Has not been affected by the current situation in recent days and is showing an upward trend. The reasons for this are: firstly, demand from the Northeast region is still strong; secondly, various factories have experienced strikes from time to time; and thirdly, the demand for military uniforms is very strong. Yesterday, over 300 pieces of 11-pound coarse cloth were traded, and all brands rose by 5 cents. Therefore, confidence is strong. Sales of fine cloth to various Northeast regions are still active. Brands such as Yanghe, Caiqiu, and Blue Double Fish have risen another 2.5 cents. However, demand from ports such as Shantou and Xiamen in Guangdong is not as strong as before, so they are slightly weaker, but asking prices have not changed much.

Eastern and Western Piece Goods 267

Have been greatly affected since the riots in Changsha. Trade with the Yangtze River region has plummeted. In addition, Eastern goods are arriving in force, causing confidence to be very weak, and prices are falling step by step. Yesterday, Huxinting fine broadcloth opened at 2 qian 4 fen 7 li 5 hao. Shuanglong shuilang continued at 2 qian 7 li 5 hao. Yang Guifei opened at 2 qian 5 li. Cute Beauty opened at 2 qian 2 li. Shuangtong deer straight tribute flannel has been sold at 2 qian 5 fen 7 li 5 hao and above. All the above prices are 2 li 5 hao less than before. Yuehua flannel, which was firm for a while, is also showing weakness. Both actual sales and local customers are quiet. Western goods are increasingly stagnant and are as rare as morning stars.

North-South Goods, New Honey Dates Arrive on the Market Yesterday 268

Tutu Sold for Twenty-Eight Taels

New honey dates from Jiaxing arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday, totaling more than 30 buckets. As the new season is just beginning, they are quite popular and the quality is good. Sales began in the market yesterday, with the tutu price opening at around 28 taels. The upper-grade merchants still followed the usual practice of adding and subtracting commissions for wholesale. As more goods are expected to arrive, the market may ease. Old stocks have been reduced and most of the sugar quality has melted and the color is also poor, so the selling price is more than ten taels different from the new goods.

Hardware, New Foreign Dollars Sell Very Well 269

New foreign dollars have been selling very well recently in the Yangtze River region, and the demand from inland Fujian merchants is also wide, so the number sold in the market in recent days has been considerable. It is heard that merchants from Tianjin, Beiping, Qingdao, and other cities have been purchasing a large number of 3-cent and 5-cent denominations in recent days. Therefore, the selling side is expected to continue to raise prices.

Construction Merchants Dump More Than 100 Tons of Deformed Steel 270

Construction merchants Feng Taixing, Xin Renji, Gongxin Factory, and other firms sold more than 160 tons of 3-cent to 1-inch deformed steel in the market yesterday. The market supply has been almost entirely purchased and the standard has a high chance of continuing to rise. The current price is 115 taels. It is heard that the public's asking price even wants to reach 120 taels.

Political Program of the Kuomintang 272

Article 6 of the Domestic Policy: Guarantee the complete freedom of assembly, association, speech, publication, residence, and belief of the people.

Article 4 of the Domestic Policy: Implement universal suffrage and abolish class elections based on wealth.

Article 7 and 8 of the Domestic Policy: Strictly determine the statutory amount of land tax and prohibit all additional levies, such as likin, which shall be abolished.

Article 12 of the Domestic Policy: Affirm the principle of equality between men and women in law, economics, education, and society, and promote the development of women's rights.

Article 9 of the Domestic Policy: Investigate household registration, reorganize cultivated land, and adjust the production and sales of food to seek equality in people's food.

Artistic Circles

The Music of Black People 296

— Yang Changxi

Black people’s contribution in music has had a wider impact than their poetry and novels, giving the world a stronger force. Not only did they give American music its Negro blood, which forms the foundation of modern American Jazz, but they also infused countries outside of America with the Negro blood of music. The Negro blood carries a crude intoxication, leading mankind towards savagery. This intense atmosphere has already conquered the people of Europe and America.

Therefore, when we discuss modern American music, or even American civilization, we cannot abandon the contributions of Black people. Furthermore, we cannot forget that Jazz, which constitutes modern American civilization, is a special symbol of the Black people’s conquest of American music and even culture. Although Jazz is just a word in the African-American language containing mixed meanings, since 1919 when Black slaves were brought to America on Dutch ships, the strong vitality of the Black people flowing within Jazz has never changed. Although there have been slight changes in form, it fundamentally cannot break free from the blood of the Black people. In the essence of Jazz, one-third is the blood of the Black people, one-third is the common American ideals and emotions of the middle class, and one-third is the spirit of the "Machine Age." Therefore, Jazz, from Africa to America, has completely conquered it. This Jazz, which has conquered over one hundred million Americans, has become America's national art, giving America its soul and national music through Jazz. Although many people believe that Jazz, which is constituted by the blood of the Black people, cannot become art and cannot last forever, Paul Whitman, who is considered the King of Jazz, believes that as long as it can appeal to the masses and touch the depths of life, it will not easily disappear in this era that is warmly welcoming it. Moreover, it did not come from Europe, nor did it originate from the palace of intellectual art, but it is a product born from the emotions of the masses. Naturally, it can surpass the evaluation of whether it is art and last forever. Therefore, while listening to Jazz, because of the natural rhythm and the fusion of emotions, people forget the constraints of the world in dance, making a powerful protest against American mechanical civilization.

In addition to Jazz, which is constituted by the blood of Black people, Black music became famous in America starting in 1871. Since the Black students' choir performed once, they were recognized by Americans. From this, because they had the opportunity to enjoy education, they slowly commanded out their original musical talent of the Black people.

The first musician who could inject the blood of the Black people into music and also boasted of it was Saint George (Chevalier Sain George 1755-1799). He was a student of Gossec, wrote two scores for violin and choir, and was also very famous in France. Similarly, August Bridgetower, who was friends with Beethoven, also praised the blood of the Black people in his songs. These two, along with Edmued Dede and Joweph White and Samuel Coleridge Taylor, were all musicians famous in Europe. However, some Black musicians in America served as singers in churches, while others served in a choir, and they could not fully represent the entire music of the Black people. Naturally, there was no talk of infusing their national blood into it. Therefore, in the past eight or ten years, the Black composers only had solo songs, violin solos, and mixed choral pieces and flute pieces, while the achievements of the singers were limited to a kind of church or affiliated group. As for musicians, only Haiy T. Buileigh had performed before the King and Queen of England and the Prince of Prussia and the Duke of Sweden, obtaining international fame, while the others did not have any great musicians.

However, the Black composers are advancing year by year, not only wanting to release a unique brilliance in American literature, but also, like novelists or poets, expressing the Black people's life and the awakening of national consciousness in their works, infusing their blood into the musical scores, so that its special qualities can forever conquer the national music of Americans. Furthermore, the Black composers in the industrial areas of northern America believe that the Black people's life in the South can be used as the basis for new melodies, and have already united with the composers and poets of the South to strive to express the Black people's life in the agricultural areas of the South. The purpose is to awaken the national consciousness in the music of all Black people in America, so that this moving power that surpasses novels can be accompanied by the increasingly prominent national consciousness in Black people's poems. In this way, Black people have entered a new dawn period in music and poetry. Let us look forward to the unfolding of new glories.

Recent Turkish Literary Circles (Continued) 297

— Ming

Turkish Wandering Poets

The poets of the Bektash sect have recently become figures in the Turkish literary scene. This is because Sadettin Nonzhel recently collected the famous works of these poets and printed them in a large book. The Bektash sect is a branch of Islam, but it is opposed to the orthodox Islamic sect, and they regard each other as enemies. Therefore, the followers of this sect created many poems and stories, striving to satirize and ridicule the orthodox religion they opposed. Because they were under the oppression of the orthodox religion, these works were secretly circulated. The founder of this sect was Hadji Bektash. It is said that he performed many miracles, and stories of these miracles have circulated among the people. There have been German translations and Old Turkish pamphlets. These stories or poems all carry a Persian flavor and Zorastrianism aura.

Fat Be

(EuadBeg), a Turkish folklorist, is collecting Turkish folk literature. Turkey has rich folk literature, but in the past, the Turks did not pay much attention to it. Only the Germans studied it in great detail. Recently, the University of Istanbul in Turkey has focused on this aspect and has a special group of people to do this work. The person in charge is Fat Be. In addition, Gross translated some Bektash stories. Gizeh and Mintzel are collecting fairy tales. Battai Gazi was a great hero in Turkish legend who defended the border of Baghdad in ancient times and prevented the invasion of the Pishanting people. There are many poems praising him in the old Turkish literature. These poems have a very strong national consciousness and fully express the national spirit. It is a pity that none of these poems have been translated into new Turkish by a new poet.

Children's Books

Has always been neglected in Turkey, so there are very few books of this kind. Because of this, the Turkish "Director of Physical Education" has also become a writer and published a small book. He calls this book "Supplementary Reading". It is full of simple and clear texts about his experiences while traveling in Europe, which is indeed a book suitable for children to read.

New Books This Year

Among them, two books are worth noting. One is "Songs and Dances of Eastern Anatolia" (SongsandDancesorEasternAnatolia) with one hundred and sixteen pages. Edited by Mahmaud Ragip and published by the Istanbul Conservatory of Music, it details the results of the Eastern Anatolian expeditions and can be regarded as a major contribution of New Turkey to the art of the Near East. Another new book is "Biography of Gazi Mustapha Kemal" by Burhan Chbit and published by Kanaat Bookstore. This is a biography of the leader of the Turkish Republic and also a history of the Turkish Republican government. It is written with great interest and the illustrations are very exquisite.

Literary Anecdotes

A Letter from Bernard Shaw 298

— Gao Lan

Refusing to Attend a Friend's Wedding

A letter written by Bernard Shaw refusing to attend the wedding of a friend has recently been revealed in Charles Grave's work "—and those Greeks". This letter was written to Grave and could have been published earlier, but it was delayed until today because of the bride's objection.

The wording of this letter is truly worthy of careful consideration. The original text is translated and published as follows:

"My dear Charles—my attending your wedding or anyone's wedding is really out of the question. In the past week, I have resolutely declined to participate in the same ceremony. If I make an exception for your affairs, I will never be able to see my good friends again.

Besides, I don't have formal attire.

I estimate that having my tailor make a suitable suit will cost me fifteen guineas (approximately 270 yuan in Chinese currency) and will be of no use to me in the future because I never wear it formally during the day. But this may be of great use to you because you rely on going out into society to earn your living. So, it is obvious that I must send you some wedding gifts. The solution to our problem is to send you this suit, thereby blessing your wedding. If I were an ordinary person,

I could give the attached check to your tailor and tell him to do his best to make you the best suit for this amount. If there is a gift book, see if he lists me in the book as "Barnett Shaw…a suit of clothes". If you want to display the gifts, the tailor shop should be able to lend you a mannequin.

I congratulate you on the passing of your youth and shake your hand with melancholy irresponsibility. I really feel sorry for Beg, but you can be sure that she is just as disappointed with anyone after a week.

As for you, it is too early to run away now. This is what you have been looking for, Charles.

Bernard Shaw"

Shanghai Market

Market News 299

Mr. Hu Dean of the Works Department of the Public Works Bureau has worked in the bureau for a long time and has a good relationship with the Chinese. Therefore, he has a wide range of contacts. He has now taken a month's leave to go to Hong Kong to escape the summer heat and set off on the 2nd. Mr. Hu has a considerable understanding of our Chinese people and had previously intended to seek a Chinese lady to marry. However, because many applicants were insincere, it did not work out. However, Mr. Hu is determined to marry a Chinese woman in the future.

Mr. Lu Songju declares that he is a legal expert, proficient in literature, and skilled in calligraphy and painting. His grandfather's works have been published and are well-known at home and abroad. He has now compiled three books that will be published soon. It is expected that there will be a large number of people who come to order them.

Guan Shengyuan declares that our company has always had the reputation of being the "King of Mooncakes". Recently, as the hot summer is about to pass, we have been actively preparing for the production of mooncakes. This year's planned scope is even wider than in previous years. In terms of promotion, there will be an organization of mooncake tea parties. The method may include giving gifts to encourage consumers to study them. Recently, our company has first produced small mooncakes for the market, divided into fruit and bean paste flavors, priced at 1.5 cents and 5 cents each. General customers are buying them very enthusiastically.

Wachang Car Company on Edward Road declares that our company's new address is located at the intersection of Zhengjia Bridge West and Hubei Road. The newly built four-story Western-style building is spacious and well-arranged. We have now moved in and are transacting business first. Once the arrangement is complete, we will officially open and hold a large sale for four weeks to reward your patronage.

Lihua Company on Nanjing Road declares that our company will hold a summer sale for 25 days starting yesterday. Our company has always been known for its low prices and high-quality goods. Therefore, customers are always more crowded every time there is a sale. All seasonal goods are also extremely sufficient. Newly arrived various satin silk pieces are specially discounted, such as printed moonlight gauze at three yards per yuan, colorfast printed hemp gauze at six to nine corners per yard, and various printed Huaer gauze, fashionable Crolo silk embroidered skirt gauze, etc. are all 50% off per yard.

New World Hotel declares that since our hotel opened the rooftop garden, we have also sold Western food and cold drinks. Travelers feel like they have entered a cool world when they enter it, so they praise it very much. The arrangement is well-made and the comfort of the travelers is fully catered for. Moreover, because the address is along the racecourse, the rooms along the western terrace are all clear and the breeze is slow and cool, especially in the summer. Paying attention to hygiene, the supplies in each room are changed every day, and the brocade quilts and gauze tents are very clean. The walls of the rooms are all cleaned with Fly-Tox, so the travelers are very enthusiastic.

Medical News 300

Yuxuan Pharmaceutical Room declares that the cough tablets secretly made by our pharmaceutical room are precisely formulated with top-quality Chinese medicines. They can stop coughs, eliminate phlegm, relieve Qi, and clear the lungs. All kinds of coughs, hoarseness, shortness of breath, phlegm asthma, pneumonia, phlegm congestion, pulmonary tuberculosis, phlegm obstruction, and various childhood coughs and pulmonary diseases are effective. All those who take them in spring will have miraculous effects after ten thousand trials. Now they are sold by Lixing Steamboat Bureau, with each box costing six bureaus.
